#HW newfunction 0
Function LibrarianA_Init
    set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 65534
    set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 455
    set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 65526
    SetModel( 21, 100 ) // LibrarianA
    CreateObject( VAR_GlobInt16_0, VAR_GlobInt16_4 )
    TurnInstant( VAR_GlobInt16_6 )
    SetStandAnimation( 2494 ) // Idle
    SetWalkAnimation( 2501 ) // Walk
    SetRunAnimation( 2501 ) // Walk
    SetLeftAnimation( 2499 ) // Turn_L
    SetRightAnimation( 2497 ) // Turn_R
    SetObjectLogicalSize( 20, 20, 30 )
    SetAnimationStandSpeed( 14, 16, 18, 20 )
    SetHeadFocusMask( 64, 1 )
    FollowFocus( 1 )
    SetObjectLogicalSize( 1, 40, 150 )
    return

#HW newfunction 8
Function LibrarianA_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 231 ) // "Shopkeeper “I know how to play cards.  Would you like to play with me?” Yes No"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 61 ) // Deck 61 - Alexandria
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 32, Field_MusicVolume ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( Field_MusicVolume == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 7, 16, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 0, 0, 0 )
        }
    } else {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 232 ) // "Shopkeeper “You can’t play if don’t have  at least 5 cards with you.”"
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    return

#HW newfunction 0
Function Nero_Init
    switch 1 ( General_FieldEntrance ) from 65534 {
    case +0:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 566
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 64982
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 47
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = 65533
        break
    default:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 65348
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 65157
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 242
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = 65529
        break
    }
    SetModel( 5500, 87 ) // Nero
    CreateObject( VAR_GlobInt16_0, VAR_GlobInt16_4 )
    TurnInstant( VAR_GlobInt16_6 )
    SetStandAnimation( 526 ) // Idle
    SetWalkAnimation( 5354 ) // Walk
    SetRunAnimation( 5351 ) // Run
    SetLeftAnimation( 5352 ) // Turn_L
    SetRightAnimation( 5353 ) // Turn_R
    SetObjectLogicalSize( 20, 20, 30 )
    SetAnimationStandSpeed( 14, 16, 18, 20 )
    SetHeadFocusMask( 96, 61 )
    EnableHeadFocus( 0 )
    return

#HW newfunction 8
Function Nero_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 268 ) // "Zenero “Let’s play a card game.” Yes No"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 10 ) // Deck 10 - Alexandria...
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 32, Field_MusicVolume ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( Field_MusicVolume == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 7, 16, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 0, 0, 0 )
        }
    } else {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 269 ) // "Zenero “You don’t have 5 cards with you.”"
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    return

Function Nero_SpeakBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_32 != 0 ) {
        set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
            DisableMove(  )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                DisableMenu(  )
            } else {
                Wait( 1 )
            }
        }
        SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
        WaitTurn(  )
        set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
        TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
        WaitTurn(  )
        RunAnimation( 8054 ) // Threten
        WindowSync( 5, 128, 234 ) // "Benero “Family is precious!”"
        WaitAnimation(  )
        set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1

            if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
                EnableMove(  )
                SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
                if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                    EnableMenu(  )
                }
            }
        }
        TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
        WaitTurn(  )
    } else {
        set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
            DisableMove(  )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                DisableMenu(  )
            } else {
                Wait( 1 )
            }
        }
        SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
        WaitTurn(  )
        set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
        TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
        WaitTurn(  )
        set VAR_GlobInt24_41 = 50
        set VAR_GlobInt16_47 = 0
        RunAnimation( 8054 ) // Threten
        SetTextVariable( 0, VAR_GlobInt24_41 )
        SetTextVariable( 7, GetGil )
        WindowSync( 5, 128, 237 ) // "Benero “Hey, it’s Zidane!  Let’s play our game!”"
        WindowAsync( 7, 0, 267 ) // "Current Funds: 0 Gil"
        WindowSync( 5, 128, 240 ) // "Benero “First, pay us 0 Gil.” Pay Don’t pay"
        WaitAnimation(  )
        if ( GetGil < VAR_GlobInt24_41 ) {
            RunAnimation( 8054 ) // Threten
            WindowSync( 5, 128, 243 ) // "Benero “Hey, you don’t have 0 Gil!”"
            CloseWindow( 7 )
            WaitAnimation(  )
            set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
                if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
                    EnableMove(  )
                    SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
                    if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                        EnableMenu(  )
                    }
                }
            }
            TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
            WaitTurn(  )
        } else {
            if ( GetDialogChoice == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobUInt8_24 = 11
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 1045, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
                RemoveGil( VAR_GlobInt24_41 )
            } else {
                CloseWindow( 7 )
                set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
                if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
                    if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
                        EnableMove(  )
                        SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
                        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                            EnableMenu(  )
                        }
                    }
                }
                TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
                WaitTurn(  )
            }
        }
    }
    return


#HW newfunction 8
Function Nero_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 270 ) // "Benero “Let’s play a card game.” Yes No"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 14 ) // Deck 14 - Alexandria
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 32, Field_MusicVolume ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( Field_MusicVolume == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 7, 16, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 0, 0, 0 )
        }
    } else {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 271 ) // "Benero “You don’t have 5 cards with you.”"
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    return

#HW newfunction 0
Function Nero_Init
    switch 1 ( General_FieldEntrance ) from 65534 {
    case +0:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 65450
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 64827
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 168
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = 65534
        break
    default:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 65526
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 64513
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 124
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = 0
        break
    }
    SetModel( 5500, 87 ) // Nero
    CreateObject( VAR_GlobInt16_0, VAR_GlobInt16_4 )
    TurnInstant( VAR_GlobInt16_6 )
    SetStandAnimation( 526 ) // Idle
    SetWalkAnimation( 5354 ) // Walk
    SetRunAnimation( 5351 ) // Run
    SetLeftAnimation( 5352 ) // Turn_L
    SetRightAnimation( 5353 ) // Turn_R
    SetObjectLogicalSize( 20, 20, 30 )
    SetAnimationStandSpeed( 14, 16, 18, 20 )
    SetHeadFocusMask( 96, 61 )
    EnableHeadFocus( 0 )
    return

#HW newfunction 3
Function Nero_SpeakBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_32 != 0 ) {
        set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
            DisableMove(  )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                DisableMenu(  )
            } else {
                Wait( 1 )
            }
        }
        SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
        WaitTurn(  )
        set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
        TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
        WaitTurn(  )
        RunAnimation( 8054 ) // Threten
        WindowSync( 6, 128, 235 ) // "Genero “We look alike, but inside,  we’re very different.”"
        WaitAnimation(  )
        set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
                EnableMove(  )
                SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
                if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                    EnableMenu(  )
                }
            }
        }
        TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
        WaitTurn(  )
    } else {
        set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
            DisableMove(  )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                DisableMenu(  )
            } else {
                Wait( 1 )
            }
        }
        SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
        WaitTurn(  )
        set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
        TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
        WaitTurn(  )
        set VAR_GlobInt24_41 = 50
        set VAR_GlobInt16_47 = 0
        RunAnimation( 8054 ) // Threten
        SetTextVariable( 0, VAR_GlobInt24_41 )
        SetTextVariable( 7, GetGil )
        WindowSync( 6, 128, 238 ) // "Genero “Hey, it’s Zidane!  Let’s play our game!”"
        WindowAsync( 7, 0, 267 ) // "Current Funds: 0 Gil"
        WindowSync( 6, 128, 241 ) // "Genero “First, pay us 0 Gil.” Pay Don’t pay"
        WaitAnimation(  )
        if ( GetGil < VAR_GlobInt24_41 ) {
            RunAnimation( 8054 ) // Threten
            WindowSync( 6, 128, 244 ) // "Genero “Hey, you don’t have 0 Gil!”"
            CloseWindow( 7 )
            WaitAnimation(  )
            set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
                if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
                    EnableMove(  )
                    SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
                    if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                        EnableMenu(  )
                    }
                }
            }
            TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
            WaitTurn(  )
        } else {
            if ( GetDialogChoice == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobUInt8_24 = 11
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 1045, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
                RemoveGil( VAR_GlobInt24_41 )
            } else {
                CloseWindow( 7 )
                set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
                if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
                    if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
                        EnableMove(  )
                        SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
                        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                            EnableMenu(  )
                        }
                    }
                }
                TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
                WaitTurn(  )
            }
        }
    }
    return


#HW newfunction 8
Function Nero_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 272 ) // "Genero “Let’s play a card game.” Yes No"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 18 ) // Deck 18 - Lindblum...
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0

#HW newfunction 13
Function Zidane_13
    TimedTurn( Angle(Treasure_PositionX, Treasure_PositionY), 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    RunAnimation( 2607 ) // Hiza_1
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 2605 ) // Hiza_2
    if ( Treasure_PickupFlag == 0 ) {
        if ( Treasure_Item == 29999 ) {
            WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
        } else {
            if ( Treasure_Item >= 1000 ) {
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                set Treasure_Gil = ( Treasure_Item - 1000 )
                if ( ( Treasure_Gil + GetGil ) > 9999999L ) {
                    set Treasure_Gil = ( 9999999L - GetGil )
                }
                AddGil( Treasure_Gil )
                SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Gil )
                WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
                set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
            } else {
                if ( ( GetItemCount(Treasure_Item) < 99 ) && ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) ) {
                    RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                    set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                    SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                    AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                    WindowSync( 7, 0, 69 ) // "  Received Item!  "
                } else {
                    if ( ( Treasure_Item >= 512 ) && ( GetCardAmount < 100 ) ) {
                        RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                        set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                        WindowSync( 7, 0, 70 ) // "  Received Item Card!  "
                    } else {
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        if ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 73 ) // "  Cannot carry another Item.  "
                        } else {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 74 ) // "  Cannot hold more Cards.  "
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    RunAnimation( 2591 ) // Hiza_3
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 200 ) // Idle
    return

#HW newfunction 12
Function Vivi_12
    EnableHeadFocus( 0 )
    TimedTurn( Angle(Treasure_PositionX, Treasure_PositionY), 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    RunAnimation( 3084 ) // Look_Up_1
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 3087 ) // Look_Up_2
    if ( Treasure_PickupFlag == 0 ) {
        if ( Treasure_Item == 29999 ) {
            WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
        } else {
            if ( Treasure_Item >= 1000 ) {
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                set Treasure_Gil = ( Treasure_Item - 1000 )
                if ( ( Treasure_Gil + GetGil ) > 9999999L ) {
                    set Treasure_Gil = ( 9999999L - GetGil )
                }
                AddGil( Treasure_Gil )
                SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Gil )
                WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
                set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
            } else {
                if ( ( GetItemCount(Treasure_Item) < 99 ) && ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) ) {
                    RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                    set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                    SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                    AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                    WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
                } else {
                    if ( ( Treasure_Item >= 512 ) && ( GetCardAmount < 100 ) ) {
                        RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                        set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                        WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
                    } else {
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        if ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 73 ) // "  Cannot carry another Item.  "
                        } else {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 74 ) // "  Cannot hold more Cards.  "
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    RunAnimation( 3092 ) // Look_Up_3
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 148 ) // Idle
    EnableHeadFocus( 3 )
    return


#HW newfunction 13
Function Vivi_13
    TimedTurn( Angle(Treasure_PositionX, Treasure_PositionY), 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    RunAnimation( 7020 ) // Hiza_1
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 7024 ) // Hiza_2
    if ( Treasure_PickupFlag == 0 ) {
        if ( Treasure_Item == 29999 ) {
            WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
        } else {
            if ( Treasure_Item >= 1000 ) {
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                set Treasure_Gil = ( Treasure_Item - 1000 )
                if ( ( Treasure_Gil + GetGil ) > 9999999L ) {
                    set Treasure_Gil = ( 9999999L - GetGil )
                }
                AddGil( Treasure_Gil )
                SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Gil )
                WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
                set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
            } else {
                if ( ( GetItemCount(Treasure_Item) < 99 ) && ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) ) {
                    RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                    set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                    SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                    AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                    WindowSync( 7, 0, 69 ) // "  Received Item!  "
                } else {
                    if ( ( Treasure_Item >= 512 ) && ( GetCardAmount < 100 ) ) {
                        RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                        set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                        WindowSync( 7, 0, 70 ) // "  Received Item Card!  "
                    } else {
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        if ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 73 ) // "  Cannot carry another Item.  "
                        } else {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 74 ) // "  Cannot hold more Cards.  "
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    RunAnimation( 7022 ) // Hiza_3
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 148 ) // Idle
    return

    loop

Function Main_Init

        set General_FieldEntrance = 10000
    }
    set General_LoadedGame = 0
    set VAR_GenInt16_9 = 355
    if ( VAR_GenUInt8_13 == 9 ) {
    } else {
        if ( ( VAR_GenUInt8_13 == 2 ) && ( VAR_GenInt16_9 < 0 ) ) {
            set VAR_GenUInt8_13 = 9
        } else {
            if ( VAR_GenInt16_9 < 0 ) {
                set VAR_GenUInt8_13 = 0
            } else {
                set VAR_GenUInt8_13 = 1
            }
        }
    }
    set VAR_GenInt16_11 = 415
    if ( VAR_GenUInt8_14 == 9 ) {
    } else {
        if ( ( VAR_GenUInt8_14 == 2 ) && ( VAR_GenInt16_11 < 0 ) ) {
            set VAR_GenUInt8_14 = 9
        } else {
            if ( VAR_GenInt16_11 < 0 ) {
                set VAR_GenUInt8_14 = 0
            } else {
                set VAR_GenUInt8_14 = 1
            }
        }
    }
    SetControlDirection( -12, -5 )
    InitCode( 2, 0 ) // Code2
    SetDialogProgression( 0 )
    switch 1 ( General_FieldEntrance ) from 65534 {
    case +0:
        set VAR_GlobUInt8_24 = 1
        InitObject( 3, 0 ) // LibrarianA
        InitObject( 4, 0 ) // Nero
        InitObject( 7, 0 ) // Nero
        InitObject( 8, 0 ) // Nero

        break
    default:
        set VAR_GenInt16_239 = 1858
        InitCode( 1, 0 ) // Code1

        set VAR_GlobUInt8_24 = 0
        if ( General_ScenarioCounter < 7100 ) {
            InitObject( 14, 0 ) // Vivi
            set VAR_GlobUInt8_32 = 1
        } else {
            InitObject( 13, 0 ) // Zidane
        }
        InitObject( 3, 0 ) // LibrarianA
        InitObject( 4, 0 ) // Nero
        InitObject( 7, 0 ) // Nero
        InitObject( 8, 0 ) // Nero
        InitRegion( 11, 0 ) // Region11
        InitRegion( 12, 0 ) // Region12
        break
    }
    InitCode( 9, 0 ) // Code9
    InitCode( 10, 0 ) // Code10
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_153 ) {
        if ( ( VAR_GlobUInt8_32 == 0 ) && ( ATE_AlexandriaBaku == 1 ) ) {
            set VAR_GlobUInt16_30 |= 1
        }
        if ( ( VAR_GlobUInt8_32 == 1 ) && ( ATE_AlexandriaTantalus == 3 ) ) {
            set VAR_GlobUInt16_30 |= 4
        }

            set VAR_GlobUInt16_30 |= 8
        }
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_153 == 1 ) {
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt16_30 != 0 ) {
                ATE( 1 )
                set VAR_GlobBool_155 = 1
                set VAR_GenInt8_238 = 1
                set VAR_GenInt16_241 = VAR_GlobUInt16_30
                if ( VAR_GenUInt16_251 != ( VAR_GenUInt16_251 | VAR_GlobUInt16_30 ) ) {
                    set VAR_GlobBool_152 = 1
                }
                set VAR_GenUInt16_251 |= VAR_GlobUInt16_30
            } else {
                ATE( 0 )
                set VAR_GlobBool_155 = 0
                set VAR_GenInt8_238 = 0
                set VAR_GenInt16_241 = 0
            }
        }
    }
    SetCameraFollowHeight( 400 )
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_158 == 0 ) {
        SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    } else {
        SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
    }
    Wait( 2 )
    Wait( 2 )
    if ( VAR_GenUInt8_13 == 9 ) {

        RaiseWindows(  )
        WaitWindow( 6 )
        set VAR_GenUInt8_14 = 0

#HW newfunction 8
Function LibrarianA_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 231 ) // "Shopkeeper “I know how to play cards.  Would you like to play with me?” Yes No"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 61 ) // Deck 61 - Alexandria
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 32, Field_MusicVolume ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( Field_MusicVolume == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 7, 16, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 0, 0, 0 )
        }
    } else {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 232 ) // "Shopkeeper “You can’t play if don’t have  at least 5 cards with you.”"
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    return

#HW newfunction 8
Function Nero_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 267 ) // "Current Funds: 0 Gil"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 10 ) // Deck 10 - Alexandria...
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 32, Field_MusicVolume ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( Field_MusicVolume == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 7, 16, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 0, 0, 0 )
        }
    } else {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 268 ) // "Zenero “Let’s play a card game.” Yes No"
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    return

#HW newfunction 8
Function Nero_CardBTN
    ifnot ( IsMovementEnabled ) {
        return
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 0
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        DisableMove(  )
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
            DisableMenu(  )
        } else {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
    }
    SetTriangleFlagMask( 127 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    set VAR_GlobUInt8_16 = GetEntryAngle(255)
    TurnTowardObject( 250, 32 ) // Player Character
    WaitTurn(  )
    if ( GetCardAmount >= 5 ) {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 269 ) // "Zenero “You don’t have 5 cards with you.”"
        if ( !GetDialogChoice ) {
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 1
            RunSoundCode3( 53248, 3105, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; [Unknown Audio]
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 48, 0 ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( 1 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 6, 24, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 255, 255, 255 )
            Wait( 25 )
            TetraMaster( 14 ) // Deck 14 - Alexandria
            set VAR_GlobBool_160 = 0
            RunSoundCode2( 34305, 0, 32, Field_MusicVolume ) // All Musics Volume Intpl ; Battle
            set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 0
            if ( Field_MusicVolume == 0 ) {
                set VAR_GlobBool_167 = 1
            }
            if ( VAR_GlobUInt8_17 == 255 ) {
                set AngleOfVector(( GetScreenCalculatedX - 160 ), ( GetScreenCalculatedY - 112 ))
            }
            CalculateScreenPosition( 250 ) // Player Character
            FadeFilter( 7, 16, VAR_GlobUInt8_17, 0, 0, 0 )
        }
    } else {
        WindowSync( 0, 128, 270 ) // "Benero “Let’s play a card game.” Yes No"
    }
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    TimedTurn( VAR_GlobUInt8_16, 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    return

#HW newfunction 0
Function Nero_Init
    switch 1 ( General_FieldEntrance ) from 65534 {
    case +0:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 65450
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 64827
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 168
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = 65534
        break
    default:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 65526
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 64513
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 124
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = 0
        break
    }
    SetModel( 5500, 87 ) // Nero
    CreateObject( VAR_GlobInt16_0, VAR_GlobInt16_4 )
    TurnInstant( VAR_GlobInt16_6 )
    SetStandAnimation( 526 ) // Idle
    SetWalkAnimation( 5354 ) // Walk
    SetRunAnimation( 5351 ) // Run
    SetLeftAnimation( 5352 ) // Turn_L
    SetRightAnimation( 5353 ) // Turn_R
    SetObjectLogicalSize( 20, 20, 30 )
    SetAnimationStandSpeed( 14, 16, 18, 20 )
    SetHeadFocusMask( 96, 61 )
    EnableHeadFocus( 0 )
    return

#HW newfunction 13
Function Zidane_13
    TimedTurn( Angle(Treasure_PositionX, Treasure_PositionY), 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    RunAnimation( 2607 ) // Hiza_1
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 2605 ) // Hiza_2
    if ( Treasure_PickupFlag == 0 ) {
        if ( Treasure_Item == 29999 ) {
            WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
        } else {
            if ( Treasure_Item >= 1000 ) {
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                set Treasure_Gil = ( Treasure_Item - 1000 )
                if ( ( Treasure_Gil + GetGil ) > 9999999L ) {
                    set Treasure_Gil = ( 9999999L - GetGil )
                }
                AddGil( Treasure_Gil )
                SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Gil )
                WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
                set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
            } else {
                if ( ( GetItemCount(Treasure_Item) < 99 ) && ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) ) {
                    RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                    set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                    SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                    AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                    WindowSync( 7, 0, 69 ) // "  Received Item!  "
                } else {
                    if ( ( Treasure_Item >= 512 ) && ( GetCardAmount < 100 ) ) {
                        RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                        set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                        WindowSync( 7, 0, 70 ) // "  Received Item Card!  "
                    } else {
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        if ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 73 ) // "  Cannot carry another Item.  "
                        } else {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 74 ) // "  Cannot hold more Cards.  "
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    RunAnimation( 2591 ) // Hiza_3
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 200 ) // Idle
    return

        while ( VAR_GlobBool_230 == 1 ) {
            Wait( 1 )
        }
        set VAR_GlobBool_231 = 1
        break
    }
    Wait( 1 )
    loop


#HW newentry 14
#HW newfunction 0
Function Vivi_Init
    switchex 2 ( General_FieldEntrance ) {
    case 831:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = VAR_GenInt16_243
        set VAR_GlobInt16_2 = VAR_GenInt16_245
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = VAR_GenInt16_247
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = VAR_GenUInt8_249
        break
    case 229:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 691
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 65496
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 32
        break
    default:
        set VAR_GlobInt16_0 = 268
        set VAR_GlobInt16_4 = 64287
        set VAR_GlobInt16_6 = 128
        break
    }
    SetModel( 8, 61 ) // Vivi
    CreateObject( VAR_GlobInt16_0, VAR_GlobInt16_4 )
    TurnInstant( VAR_GlobInt16_6 )
    SetStandAnimation( 148 ) // Idle
    SetWalkAnimation( 571 ) // Walk
    SetRunAnimation( 419 ) // Run
    SetLeftAnimation( 917 ) // Turn_L
    SetRightAnimation( 918 ) // Turn_R
    SetInactiveAnimation( 912 ) // Break1
    SetObjectLogicalSize( 20, 30, 44 )
    SetAnimationStandSpeed( 14, 16, 18, 20 )
    SetHeadFocusMask( 65, 57 )
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 912 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 914 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunModelCode( 16, 571, 4, 912 ) // Add Sound
    RunModelCode( 17, 571, 4, 914 ) // Add Secondary Sound
    RunModelCode( 18, 571, 4, 1 ) // Sound Random Pitch
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 912 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 914 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunModelCode( 16, 571, 14, 912 ) // Add Sound
    RunModelCode( 17, 571, 14, 914 ) // Add Secondary Sound
    RunModelCode( 18, 571, 14, 1 ) // Sound Random Pitch
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 912 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 914 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunModelCode( 16, 419, 0, 912 ) // Add Sound
    RunModelCode( 17, 419, 0, 914 ) // Add Secondary Sound
    RunModelCode( 18, 419, 0, 1 ) // Sound Random Pitch
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 912 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunSoundCode( 4616, 914 ) // Sound Null ; [Unknown Audio]
    RunModelCode( 16, 419, 9, 912 ) // Add Sound
    RunModelCode( 17, 419, 9, 914 ) // Add Secondary Sound
    RunModelCode( 18, 419, 9, 1 ) // Sound Random Pitch
    DefinePlayerCharacter(  )
    set VAR_GlobBool_158 = 1
    if ( VAR_GlobBool_159 == 1 ) {
        if ( VAR_GlobBool_156 == 0 ) {
            EnableMove(  )
            SetTriangleFlagMask( 255 )
            if ( VAR_GlobBool_144 == 0 ) {
                EnableMenu(  )
            }
        }
    }
    return

#HW newfunction 12
Function Vivi_12
    EnableHeadFocus( 0 )
    TimedTurn( Angle(Treasure_PositionX, Treasure_PositionY), 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    RunAnimation( 3084 ) // Look_Up_1
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 3087 ) // Look_Up_2
    if ( Treasure_PickupFlag == 0 ) {
        if ( Treasure_Item == 29999 ) {
            WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
        } else {
            if ( Treasure_Item >= 1000 ) {
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                set Treasure_Gil = ( Treasure_Item - 1000 )
                if ( ( Treasure_Gil + GetGil ) > 9999999L ) {
                    set Treasure_Gil = ( 9999999L - GetGil )
                }
                AddGil( Treasure_Gil )
                SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Gil )
                WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
                set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
            } else {
                if ( ( GetItemCount(Treasure_Item) < 99 ) && ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) ) {
                    RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                    set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                    SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                    AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                    WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
                } else {
                    if ( ( Treasure_Item >= 512 ) && ( GetCardAmount < 100 ) ) {
                        RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                        set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                        WindowSync( 7, 0, 104 ) // " =  Recruiting New Knights of Pluto Members  =  We are always looking for recruits for the Knights of Pluto in Alexandria Castle! Come, all you brave young men! Let us protect the queen, and our beautiful country, together!                      Captain, Knights of Pluto "
                    } else {
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        if ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 73 ) // "  Cannot carry another Item.  "
                        } else {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 74 ) // "  Cannot hold more Cards.  "
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    RunAnimation( 3092 ) // Look_Up_3
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 148 ) // Idle
    EnableHeadFocus( 3 )
    return


#HW newfunction 13
Function Vivi_13
    TimedTurn( Angle(Treasure_PositionX, Treasure_PositionY), 16 )
    WaitTurn(  )
    RunAnimation( 7020 ) // Hiza_1
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 7024 ) // Hiza_2
    if ( Treasure_PickupFlag == 0 ) {
        if ( Treasure_Item == 29999 ) {
            WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
        } else {
            if ( Treasure_Item >= 1000 ) {
                RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                set Treasure_Gil = ( Treasure_Item - 1000 )
                if ( ( Treasure_Gil + GetGil ) > 9999999L ) {
                    set Treasure_Gil = ( 9999999L - GetGil )
                }
                AddGil( Treasure_Gil )
                SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Gil )
                WindowSync( 7, 0, 71 ) // "  Received 0 Gil!  "
                set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
            } else {
                if ( ( GetItemCount(Treasure_Item) < 99 ) && ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) ) {
                    RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                    set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                    SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                    AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                    WindowSync( 7, 0, 69 ) // "  Received Item!  "
                } else {
                    if ( ( Treasure_Item >= 512 ) && ( GetCardAmount < 100 ) ) {
                        RunSoundCode3( 53248, 108, 0, -128, 125 ) // Play Sound ; South Gate
                        set Treasure_PickupFlag = 1
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        AddItem( Treasure_Item, 1 )
                        WindowSync( 7, 0, 70 ) // "  Received Item Card!  "
                    } else {
                        SetTextVariable( 0, Treasure_Item )
                        if ( Treasure_Item < 512 ) {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 73 ) // "  Cannot carry another Item.  "
                        } else {
                            WindowSync( 7, 0, 74 ) // "  Cannot hold more Cards.  "
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    RunAnimation( 7022 ) // Hiza_3
    WaitAnimation(  )
    SetStandAnimation( 148 ) // Idle
    return


#HW newfunction 1
Function Vivi_Loop
    Wait( 1 )
    loop
